[30;1m38 | [0m[35m## Interval operations[0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35mKey genomic interval operations in bioframe include:[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35m- `overlap`: Find pairs of overlapping genomic intervals between two dataframes.[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35m- `closest`: For every interval in a dataframe, find the closest intervals in a second dataframe.[0m
[30;1m43 | [0m[35m- `cluster`: Group overlapping intervals in a dataframe into clusters.[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35m- `complement`: Find genomic intervals that are not covered by any interval from a dataframe.[0m
